  <!-- /吸顶 分享按钮 -->
      <script type="text/javascript">
        //吸顶效果
            (function(){
              function getByClass(oParent,sClass){
                  if(oParent){
                    if(oParent.getElementsByClassName){
                      return oParent.getElementsByClassName(sClass);
                    }else{
                      var arr=[];
                      var reg=new RegExp("\\b"+sClass+"\\b");
                      var aEle=document.getElementsByTagName("*");
                      for(var i=0;i<aEle.length;i++){
                        if(reg.test(aEle[i].className)){
                          arr.push(aEle[i]);
                        }
                      }
                      return arr;
                    }
                  }else{
                    console.log("父级无效元素");
                  }
              }
              function getPos(obj){
                  var t = 0;
                  while(obj){
                      t+=obj.offsetTop;
                      obj = obj.offsetParent;
                  }
                  return t;
              }
              function addEvent(obj,sEv,fn){
                if(obj.addEventListener){
                  obj.addEventListener(sEv,function(ev){
                    var oEvent=ev || event;
                    if(fn.apply(obj,arguments)==false){
                      oEvent.cancelBubble=true;
                      oEvent.preventDefault();
                    }
                  },false);
                }else{
                  obj.attachEvent('on'+sEv,function(ev){
                    var oEvent=ev || event;
                    if(fn.apply(obj,arguments)==false){
                      oEvent.cancelBubble=true;
                      return false; 
                    }
                  });
                }
              }

                $(function(){
                  var isIE6=window.navigator.userAgent.indexOf("MSIE 6.0");
                  if(isIE6!=-1){
                    return;
                  }
                
                  function setTitle(){
                    var navTitle=document.getElementById("smallBodyTitle");

                    var artibodyTitle=document.getElementById('artibodyTitle').innerHTML;
                    navTitle.innerHTML=artibodyTitle;
                    if(!navTitle.innerHTML){
                      setTitle();
                    }
                  }
                  setTitle();

                  function setComment(){
                    var commentCount1=document.getElementById("commentCount1").innerHTML;
                    var commentCount1M=document.getElementById("commentCount1M");
                    commentCount1M.innerHTML=commentCount1;
                    if(!commentCount1){
                      var time;
                      clearTimeout(time);
                      time=setTimeout(function(){
                         setComment();
                      },500);
                    }
                  }
                  setComment();

                  var pageToolShare=document.getElementById("pageToolShare");
                  var showC=false;
                  pageToolShare.onclick=function(){
                    if(showC){
                      $("#wrapOuter").removeClass("show-comment");
                      $("body").removeClass("page-1260");
                      showC=false;
                    }else{
                      $("#wrapOuter").addClass("show-comment");
                      $("body").addClass("page-1260");
                      showC=true;
                    }
                  };

                  var erweima=getByClass(document,"news_weixin_ercode")[0];
                  var navStopHere=document.getElementById("navStopHere")||erweima;

                  var navTop2=document.getElementById("page-info2");

                  var offsetH=getPos(navStopHere)+20;
                  var scrollHeight=0;

                  addEvent(window,"load",function(){
                      offsetH=getPos(navStopHere)+20;
                  })

                  addEvent(window,"scroll",function(){

                    scrollHeight=document.documentElement.scrollTop||document.body.scrollTop;
                    if(scrollHeight>=350&&scrollHeight<=offsetH){
                      navTop2.style.display="block";
                    }else if(scrollHeight<350){
                      navTop2.style.display="none";
                    }else if(scrollHeight>offsetH){
                      navTop2.style.display="none";
                    }
                  });
                });
            })();
      </script>

        <div class="article article_16" id="artibody">

			


					
	<p>　　原标题：电影《侏罗纪公园》大反派饰演者涉嫌性侵女童被判6年</p>
<p>　　中新社旧金山4月27日电 涉嫌在家辅导时伺机多次性侵13岁女学生的美国影视表演教师、演员卡梅伦·托尔27日在加州被判6年监禁，并终身登记为性犯罪者。托尔曾在电影《侏罗纪公园》里扮演大反派刘易斯·道奇森，也出演过《星际迷航：下一代》等。</p>
<div id="ad_44089" class="otherContent_01" style="display: block; margin: 10px 20px 10px 0px; float: left; overflow: hidden; clear: both; padding: 4px; width: 300px; height: 250px;"><ins class="sinaads sinaads-done" id="Sinads49447" data-ad-pdps="PDPS000000044089" data-ad-status="done" data-ad-offset-left="0" data-ad-offset-top="0" style="display: block; overflow: hidden; text-decoration: none;"><ins style="text-decoration:none;margin:0px auto;width:300px;display:block;position:relative;"><iframe width="300px" height="250px" frameborder="0" marginwidth="0" marginheight="0" vspace="0" hspace="0" allowtransparency="true" scrolling="no" src="http://x.jd.com/exsites?spread_type=2&amp;ad_ids=1884:5&amp;location_info=0&amp;callback=getjjsku_callback" name="clickTAG=http%3A%2F%2Fsax.sina.com.cn%2Fmfp%2Fclick%3Ftype%3D3%26t%3DMjAxNi0wNC0yOSAyMTowMTo0OAkxMTMuMjUwLjE1NS43OAkxMTMuMjUxLjE2NS4yMjdfMTQ2MTIyNTYwMy45MDQ5OTEJaHR0cDovL25ld3Muc2luYS5jb20uY24vby8yMDE2LTA0LTI4L2RvYy1pZnhydWFlZTQ5ODg5MTAuc2h0bWwJUERQUzAwMDAwMDA0NDA4OQk1NzJjNTBmZi1mNTBlLTQ5MGYtYTFiZC0wNGEzNmU2YjY4NjUJMDRDQ0I2Mzc3QkQ2CTA0Q0NCNjM3N0JENgl1c2VyX2dyb3VwOjkwOCw5MDcsOTAzLDkwMXx1c2VyX3RhZzoyMDk1MSwyMDk1OSwyMDk1MywyMDg0NywyMDEwNywyMTE2NywyMDk1MiwyMTA2MCwyMTM3NywyMTI3MHxwb3M6UERQUzAwMDAwMDA0NDA4OXx3YXBfb3M6NzAzfHZfaXNwOjEzMDB8dXNlcl9hZ2U6NjA1LDYwNiw2MDF8dl96b25lOjMwMzAwMCwzMDMwMDB8dXNlcl9nZW5kZXI6NTAyfF92X3pvbmU6MzAzMDAwLDMwMzAwMHxtb2JpbGVfYnJhbmQ6MTIwOXxtb2JpbGVfYnJvd3Nlcjo4MTF8dmVyc2lvbjpnbF9icDFfMQkJMzAzMDAwfDMwMzAwMAk1NjBBREU3RTBEQzMJTFkxNTEyMDk2NQlQRFBTMDAwMDAwMDQ0MDg5CTU2MEFERTdFMERDM19wb3J0YWwJQUUJLQk4CS0JLQktCS0JLQktCS0JLQkyCTE0CXN0cmF0ZWd5X2RlZmF1bHQJMAk2CWNvbnRyYWN0OjAsMw%253D%253D&amp;viewTAG=http%3A%2F%2Fsax.sina.com.cn%2Fmfp%2Fview%3Ftype%3D3%26t%3DMjAxNi0wNC0yOSAyMTowMTo0OAkxMTMuMjUwLjE1NS43OAkxMTMuMjUxLjE2NS4yMjdfMTQ2MTIyNTYwMy45MDQ5OTEJaHR0cDovL25ld3Muc2luYS5jb20uY24vby8yMDE2LTA0LTI4L2RvYy1pZnhydWFlZTQ5ODg5MTAuc2h0bWwJUERQUzAwMDAwMDA0NDA4OQk1NzJjNTBmZi1mNTBlLTQ5MGYtYTFiZC0wNGEzNmU2YjY4NjUJMDRDQ0I2Mzc3QkQ2CTA0Q0NCNjM3N0JENgl1c2VyX2dyb3VwOjkwOCw5MDcsOTAzLDkwMXx1c2VyX3RhZzoyMDk1MSwyMDk1OSwyMDk1MywyMDg0NywyMDEwNywyMTE2NywyMDk1MiwyMTA2MCwyMTM3NywyMTI3MHxwb3M6UERQUzAwMDAwMDA0NDA4OXx3YXBfb3M6NzAzfHZfaXNwOjEzMDB8dXNlcl9hZ2U6NjA1LDYwNiw2MDF8dl96b25lOjMwMzAwMCwzMDMwMDB8dXNlcl9nZW5kZXI6NTAyfF92X3pvbmU6MzAzMDAwLDMwMzAwMHxtb2JpbGVfYnJhbmQ6MTIwOXxtb2JpbGVfYnJvd3Nlcjo4MTF8dmVyc2lvbjpnbF9icDFfMQkJMzAzMDAwfDMwMzAwMAk1NjBBREU3RTBEQzMJTFkxNTEyMDk2NQlQRFBTMDAwMDAwMDQ0MDg5CTU2MEFERTdFMERDM19wb3J0YWwJQUUJLQk4CS0JLQktCS0JLQktCS0JLQkyCTE0CXN0cmF0ZWd5X2RlZmF1bHQJMAk2CWNvbnRyYWN0OjAsMw%253D%253D%26userid%3D113.251.165.227_1461225603.904991%26viewlog%3Dfalse"></iframe></ins></ins></div><p>　　综合《洛杉矶时报》、美国广播公司等媒体报道，56岁的托尔和妻子经营影视表演培训学校，经他辅导过的演员包括一线影星卡梅伦·迪亚兹、奥斯卡最佳女主角海伦·亨特以及歌星麦当娜等。</p>
<p>　　2014年6月，一名加州大学洛杉矶分校女学生提起诉讼，称2008年4月至2009年3月间，托尔在其位于山上的家中为她提供私人辅导课，在山路上驾驶时给她吸食大麻，并多次将其强暴，当时她年仅13岁。</p>
<p>　　托尔被捕，被控14项对14岁以下儿童实施绑架、抢劫、强暴和性犯罪等罪名，保释金260万美元。</p>
<p>　　案件进入审理阶段后，托尔的13项罪名被取消，陪审团认定其一项猥亵儿童罪。</p>
<p>　　今年4月27日，洛杉矶高等法院法官马丁·赫斯卡维斯宣布对托尔监禁6年的刑事判决，并谴责他利用受害人的弱小无助，策划了犯罪行为。</p>
<p>　　在法官宣布判决前，受害人出庭宣读她的书面声明，请求法官对托尔处以最高刑罚。</p>
<p>　　托尔的辩护律师马克·拉格斯当天说，他的当事人被冤枉，他很乐观地预计案件最终一定会逆转。（完）</p>

          <p>什么叫文化的隔膜？本来我以为自己跟台湾人没有什么文化隔膜，都是中国人，说中国话，彼此之间也没什么矛盾。但是后来我发现了，所谓文化的隔膜和差异，就是聊天聊半小时到一小时以后，找不到词了。</p>

          <p>政治家都爱吹牛，反正吹牛也不上税。所以美国有句俗话，世界上最不靠谱的，就是政治家当选前的承诺，还有男人婚前的誓言。所以，从这个角度看，每个男人都是天生的政治家。</p>
